Complete All Speedtest IP Address List - Mikrotik Script

Complete All Speed Test IP Address List

So that it is not heavy when entering the address via the new terminal, first create a file with the extension rsc, then enter it in the file in mkrotik next import the script with the command "export file = speedtest.rsc"

/ip firewall address-list
